&ldquo;ChIPseeker: an R/Bioconductor package for ChIP peak annotation, comparison and visualization.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>31</b>(14), pp. 2382-2383.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btv145">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btv145</a>. 
</p>

---------
chipseq
<p>Sarkar D, Gentleman R, Lawrence M and Yao Z (2016).
<em>chipseq: chipseq: A package for analyzing chipseq data</em>.
R package version 1.24.0. 
</p>

---------
ChIPseqR
<p>Humburg P, Helliwell C, Bulger D and Stone G (2011).
&ldquo;ChIPseqR: Analysis of ChIP-seq Experiments.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>, <b>12</b>(1), pp. 39.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1186/1471-2105-12-39">doi: 10.1186/1471-2105-12-39</a>, <a href="http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/12/39">http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/12/39</a>. 
</p>

---------
ChIPsim
<p>Humburg P (2011).
<em>ChIPsim: Simulation of ChIP-seq experiments</em>.
R package version 1.28.0. 
</p>

---------
ChIPXpress
<p>Wu G (2012).
<em>ChIPXpress: ChIPXpress: enhanced transcription factor target gene
identification from ChIP-seq and ChIP-chip data using publicly
available gene expression profiles</em>.
R package version 1.16.0. 
</p>

---------
chopsticks
<p>Leung H (2015).
<em>chopsticks: The snp.matrix and X.snp.matrix classes</em>.
R package version 1.38.0, <a href="http://outmodedbonsai.sourceforge.net/">http://outmodedbonsai.sourceforge.net/</a>. 
</p>

---------
chroGPS
<p>Reina O and Rossell D (2016).
<em>chroGPS: chroGPS: visualizing the epigenome</em>.
R package version 1.22.0. 
</p>

---------
chromDraw
<p>Janecka J and Lysak MA (2015).
&ldquo;chromDraw: an R package for visualization of linear and circular karyotypes.&rdquo;
<em>Chromosome Research</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1007/s10577-015-9513-5">doi: 10.1007/s10577-015-9513-5</a>, <a href="http://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s10577-015-9513-5">http://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s10577-015-9513-5</a>. 
</p>

---------
ChromHeatMap
<p>Rayner TF (2016).
<em>ChromHeatMap: Heat map plotting by genome coordinate</em>.
R package version 1.28.0. 
</p>

---------
chromPlot
<p>Verdugo RA and Orostica KY (2016).
<em>chromPlot: Global visualization tool of genomic data</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
chromstaR
<p>Taudt A, Nguyen MA, Heinig M, Johannes F and Colome-Tatche M (2016).
&ldquo;chromstaR: Tracking combinatorial chromatin state dynamics in space and time.&rdquo;
<em>bioRxiv</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1101/038612">doi: 10.1101/038612</a>, <a href="http://dx.doi.org/10.1101/038612">http://dx.doi.org/10.1101/038612</a>. 
</p>

---------
CHRONOS
<p>Vrahatis AG, Dimitrakopoulou K, Balomenos P, Tsakalidis A and Bezerianos A (2016).
&ldquo;CHRONOS: A time-varying method for microRNA-mediated sub-pathway enrichment analysis.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>32</b>(6), pp. 884-892. 
</p>

---------
CINdex
<p>Song L, Bhuvaneshwar K, Wang Y, Feng Y, Shih I, Madhavan S and Gusev Y (2016).
<em>CINdex: Chromosome Instability Index</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
cisPath
<p>Wang L (2016).
<em>cisPath: Visualization and management of the protein-protein interaction
networks.</em>.
R package version 1.14.0. 
</p>

---------
ClassifyR
<p>Strbenac D, Mann GJ, Ormerod JT and Yang JYH (2015).
&ldquo;ClassifyR: an R package for performance assessment of classification with applications to transcriptomics.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>31</b>(11), pp. 1851-1853. 
</p>

---------
cleanUpdTSeq
<p>Sheppard S, Lawson N and Zhu L (2013).
&ldquo;Accurate identification of polyadenylation sites from 3' end deep 
sequencing using a naive Bayes classifier.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>29</b>(20), pp. 2564.
ISSN 1460-2059, <a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btt446">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btt446</a>, <a href="http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/29/20/2564.long">http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/29/20/2564.long</a>. 
</p>

---------
cleaver
<p>Gibb S (2015).
<em>cleaver: Cleavage of Polypeptide Sequences</em>.
R package version 1.12.0, <a href="https://github.com/sgibb/cleaver/">https://github.com/sgibb/cleaver/</a>.

R package version 1.14.0. 
</p>

Clomial
<p>Zare, H and al. e (2014).

</p>

<em>Clonality: Clonality testing</em>.
R package version 1.22.0. 
</p>

clonotypeR

&ldquo;clonotypeR&ndash;high throughput analysis of T cell antigen receptor sequences.&rdquo;
<em>bioRxiv</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1101/028696">doi: 10.1101/028696</a>, http://www.biorxiv.org/content/early/2015/10/08/028696.full.pdf, <a href="http://www.biorxiv.org/content/early/2015/10/08/028696">http://www.biorxiv.org/content/early/2015/10/08/028696</a>. 
</p>

R package version 1.22.0. 
</p>

R package version 1.22.0. 
</p>

R package version 1.2.1.

R package version 1.0.0.

<em>OMICS: A Journal of Integrative Biology</em>, <b>16</b>(5), pp. 284-287.

</p>

ClusterSignificance

R package version 1.2.0.

&ldquo;DiffLogo: a comparative visualization of sequence motifs.&rdquo;
<em>BMC bioinformatics</em>, <b>16</b>.
ISSN 1471&ndash;2105, <a href="http://bmcbioinformatics.biomedcentral.com/articles/10.1186/s12859-015-0767-x">http://bmcbioinformatics.biomedcentral.com/articles/10.1186/s12859-015-0767-x</a>. 
</p>

Director
<p>Icay K (2016).

R package version 1.0.0, <a href="https://github.com/kzouchka/Director">https://github.com/kzouchka/Director</a>. 
</p>

R package version 1.16.0. 
</p>

R package version 1.20.0.

R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

<em>Epigenetics &amp; Chromatin</em>, <b>8</b>, pp. 6.
<a href="http://www.epigeneticsandchromatin.com/content/8/1/6">http://www.epigeneticsandchromatin.com/content/8/1/6</a>.

flowMap
<p>Chiaowen Joyce Hsiao, Yu
Qian and Richard H.
Scheuermann (2016).
<em>flowMap: Mapping cell populations in flow cytometry data for cross-sample
comparisons using the Friedman-Rafsky Test</em>.
R package version 1.12.0. 
</p>

R package version 1.10.0.

<p>Arora S, Morgan M, Carlson M and PagÃ¨s H (2016).
<em>GenomeInfoDb: Utilities for manipulating chromosome and other 'seqname'
identifiers</em>.
R package version 1.10.1. 
</p>

---------
genomeIntervals
<p>Gagneur J, Toedling J, Bourgon R and Delhomme N (2015).
<em>genomeIntervals: Operations on genomic intervals</em>.
R package version 1.30.0. 
</p>

genomes
<p>Stubben C (2015).
<em>genomes: Genome sequencing project metadata</em>.
R package version 3.4.0. 
</p>

---------
GenomicAlignments
<p>Lawrence M, Huber W, PagÃ¨s H, Aboyoun P, Carlson M, Gentleman R, Morgan M and Carey V (2013).
&ldquo;Software for Computing and Annotating Genomic Ranges.&rdquo;
<em>PLoS Computational Biology</em>, <b>9</b>.

---------
GenomicFeatures
<p>Lawrence M, Huber W, PagÃ¨s H, Aboyoun P, Carlson M, Gentleman R, Morgan M and Carey V (2013).
&ldquo;Software for Computing and Annotating Genomic Ranges.&rdquo;
<em>PLoS Computational Biology</em>, <b>9</b>.

---------
GenomicFiles
<p>Bioconductor Package Maintainer, Obenchain V, Love M, Shepherd L and Morgan M (2016).

R package version 1.10.3. 
</p>

---------
GenomicInteractions
<p>Harmston, N., Ing-Simmons, E., Perry, M., Baresic, A., Lenhard and B. (2015).
<em>GenomicInteractions: R package for handling genomic interaction data</em>.
R package version 1.8.0, <a href="https://github.com/ComputationalRegulatoryGenomicsICL/GenomicInteractions/">https://github.com/ComputationalRegulatoryGenomicsICL/GenomicInteractions/</a>.

---------
GenomicRanges
<p>Lawrence M, Huber W, PagÃ¨s H, Aboyoun P, Carlson M, Gentleman R, Morgan M and Carey V (2013).

<em>PLoS Computational Biology</em>, <b>9</b>.

&ldquo;Representation and Manipulation of Genomic Tuples in R.&rdquo;

<a href="http://doi.org/10.21105/joss.00020">doi: 10.21105/joss.00020</a>, <a href="http://joss.theoj.org/papers/64b99f363d24b8a7e9025188183e9865">http://joss.theoj.org/papers/64b99f363d24b8a7e9025188183e9865</a>.

---------
genoset
<p>Haverty PM (2016).
<em>genoset: A RangedSummarizedExperiment with methods for copy number
analysis</em>.
R package version 1.30.0, <a href="https://github.com/phaverty/genoset">https://github.com/phaverty/genoset</a>. 
</p>

---------
genotypeeval
<p>Tom J (2016).
<em>genotypeeval: QA/QC of a gVCF or VCF file</em>.
R package version 1.4.0. 
</p>

---------
genphen
<p>Kitanovski S (2016).
<em>genphen: A tool for computing genotype-phenotype associations
using statistical learning techniques</em>.
University Duisburg-Essen,  Essen, Germany.
R package version 1.0, <a href="http://www.bioconductor.org/packages/release/genphen.html">http://www.bioconductor.org/packages/release/genphen.html</a>. 
</p>

---------
GenRank
<p>Kanduri C (2016).
<em>GenRank: Candidate gene prioritization based on convergent evidence</em>.
R package version 1.2.0, <a href="https://github.com/chakri9/GenRank">https://github.com/chakri9/GenRank</a>. 
</p>

---------
GenVisR
<p>Skidmore ZL, Wagner AH, Lesurf R, Campbell KM, Kunisaki J, Griffith OL and Griffith M (2016).
&ldquo;GenVisR: Genomic Visualizations in R.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>. 
</p>

---------
GEOmetadb
<p>Zhu Y, Davis S, Stephens R, Meltzer PS and Chen Y (2008).
&ldquo;GEOmetadb: powerful alternative search engine for the Gene Expression Omnibus.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics (Oxford, England)</em>, <b>24</b>(23), pp. 2798&ndash;2800.
ISSN 1367-4811, <a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btn520">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btn520</a>, <a href="http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/18842599">http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/18842599</a>. 
</p>

---------
GEOquery
<p>Davis S and Meltzer P (2007).
&ldquo;GEOquery: a bridge between the Gene Expression Omnibus (GEO) and BioConductor.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>14</b>, pp. 1846&ndash;1847. 
</p>

---------
GEOsearch
<p>Ji Z and Ji H (2015).
<em>GEOsearch: GEOsearch</em>.
R package version 1.0.0. 
</p>

---------
GEOsubmission
<p>Kuhn A (2010).
<em>GEOsubmission: Prepares microarray data for submission to GEO</em>.
R package version 1.26.0. 
</p>

---------
gespeR
<p>Schmich F (2015).
<em>gespeR: Gene-Specific Phenotype EstimatoR</em>.
R package version 1.6.0, <a href="http://www.cbg.ethz.ch/software/gespeR">http://www.cbg.ethz.ch/software/gespeR</a>. 
</p>

---------
GEWIST
<p>Deng WQ and Pare G (2016).
<em>GEWIST: Gene Environment Wide Interaction Search Threshold</em>.
R package version 1.18.0. 
</p>

---------
GGBase
<p>Carey V (2016).
<em>GGBase: GGBase infrastructure for genetics of gene expression package
GGtools</em>.
R package version 3.36.0. 
</p>

---------
ggbio
<p>Yin T, Cook D and Lawrence M (2012).
&ldquo;ggbio: an R package for extending the grammar of graphics for genomic data.&rdquo;
<em>Genome Biology</em>, <b>13</b>(8), pp. R77. 
</p>

---------
ggcyto
<p>Jiang M (2015).
<em>ggcyto: Visualize Cytometry data with ggplot</em>.
R package version 1.2.1, <a href="https://github.com/RGLab/ggcyto/issues">https://github.com/RGLab/ggcyto/issues</a>. 
</p>

---------
GGtools
<p>Carey VJ, Davis AR, Lawrence MF, Gentleman R and Raby BA (2009).
&ldquo;Data structures and algorithms for analysis of genetics of gene expression with Bioconductor: GGtools 3.x.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>25</b>(11), pp. 1447&ndash;8.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btp169">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btp169</a>, <a href="http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/25/11/1447.long">http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/25/11/1447.long</a>. 
</p>

---------
ggtree
<p>Yu G, Smith D, Zhu H, Guan Y and Lam TT (accepted).
&ldquo;ggtree: an R package for visualization and annotation of phylogenetic trees with their covariates and other associated data.&rdquo;
<em>Methods in Ecology and Evolution</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1111/2041-210X.12628">doi: 10.1111/2041-210X.12628</a>. 
</p>

---------
girafe
<p>Toedling J, Ciaudo C, Voinnet O, Heard E and Barillot E (2010).
&ldquo;girafe - an R/Bioconductor package for functional exploration of aligned next-generation sequencing reads.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>26</b>, pp. 2902-2903.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btq531">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btq531</a>. 
</p>

---------
GLAD
<p>Hupe P (2011).
<em>GLAD: Gain and Loss Analysis of DNA</em>.
R package version 2.38.0, <a href="http://bioinfo.curie.fr">http://bioinfo.curie.fr</a>. 
</p>

---------
Glimma
<p>Su S, Ritchie M and Law C (2016).
<em>Glimma: Interactive HTML graphics</em>.
R package version 1.2.1, <a href="https://github.com/Shians/Glimma">https://github.com/Shians/Glimma</a>. 
</p>

---------
GlobalAncova
<p>Mansmann U, Meister R, Hummel M, Scheufele R and Knueppel wcfS (2010).
<em>GlobalAncova: Calculates a global test for differential gene expression
between groups</em>.
R package version 3.42.0. 
</p>

---------
globalSeq
<p>Rauschenberger A, Jonker MA, van de Wiel MA and Menezes RX (2016).
&ldquo;Testing for association between RNA-Seq and high-dimensional data.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>, <b>17:118</b>.
<a href="http://dx.doi.org/10.1186/s12859-016-0961-5">http://dx.doi.org/10.1186/s12859-016-0961-5</a>. 
</p>

---------
globaltest
<p>Goeman JJ and Oosting J (2016).
<em>Globaltest: testing association of a group of genes
with a clinical variable</em>.
R package version 5.28.0. 
</p>

<p>Goeman JJ, van de Geer SA and van Houwelingen JC (2006).
&ldquo;Testing against a high-dimensional alternative.&rdquo;
<em>Journal of the Royal Statistical Society, Series B</em>, pp. 477-493. 
</p>

<p>Goeman JJ, van de Geer SA, de Kort F and van Houwelingen JC (2004).
&ldquo;A global test for groups of genes: testing
association with a clinical outcome.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, pp. 93-99. 
</p>

---------
gmapR
<p>Barr C, Wu T and Lawrence M (2016).
<em>gmapR: An R interface to the GMAP/GSNAP/GSTRUCT suite</em>.
R package version 1.16.0. 
</p>

---------
GMRP
<p>Tan Y and Liu D (2015).
<em>GMRP: GWAS-based Mendelian Randomization and Path Analyses</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
GOexpress
<p>Rue-Albrecht K (2016).
<em>GOexpress: Visualise microarray and RNAseq data using gene ontology
annotations</em>.
R package version 1.8.0, <a href="https://github.com/kevinrue/GOexpress">https://github.com/kevinrue/GOexpress</a>. 
</p>

---------
GOFunction
<p>Wang J (2013).
<em>GOFunction: GO-function: deriving biologcially relevant functions from
statistically significant functions</em>.
R package version 1.22.0. 
</p>

---------
GoogleGenomics
<p>Doll C, Deflaux N and Bagaria S (2015).
<em>GoogleGenomics: R Client for Google Genomics API</em>.
R package version 1.6.0, <a href="https://cloud.google.com/genomics/">https://cloud.google.com/genomics/</a>. 
</p>

---------
GOpro
<p>Chrabaszcz L (2016).
<em>GOpro: Find the most characteristic gene ontology terms for groups of
human genes</em>.
R package version 1.0.0, <a href="https://github.com/mi2-warsaw/GOpro">https://github.com/mi2-warsaw/GOpro</a>. 
</p>

---------
goProfiles
<p>Sanchez A, Ocana J and Salicru M (2016).
<em>goProfiles: goProfiles: an R package for the statistical analysis of
functional profiles</em>.
R package version 1.36.0. 
</p>

---------
GOSemSim
<p>Yu G, Li F, Qin Y, Bo X, Wu Y and Wang S (2010).
&ldquo;GOSemSim: an R package for measuring semantic similarity among GO terms and gene products.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>26</b>(7), pp. 976-978.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btq064">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btq064</a>.

---------
goseq
<p>Young MD, Wakefield MJ, Smyth GK and Oshlack A (2010).
&ldquo;Gene ontology analysis for RNA-seq: accounting for selection bias.&rdquo;
<em>Genome Biology</em>, <b>11</b>, pp. R14. 
</p>

---------
GOstats
<p>Falcon S and Gentleman R (2007).
&ldquo;Using GOstats to test gene lists for GO term association.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>23</b>(2), pp. 257-8. 
</p>

---------
GOsummaries
<p>Kolde R (2016).
<em>GOsummaries: Word cloud summaries of GO enrichment analysis</em>.
R package version 2.8.0, <a href="https://github.com/raivokolde/GOsummaries">https://github.com/raivokolde/GOsummaries</a>. 
</p>

---------
GOTHiC
<p>Mifsud B and Sugar R (2013).
<em>GOTHiC: Binomial test for Hi-C data analysis</em>.
R package version 1.10.0. 
</p>

---------
goTools
<p>Yang YH and Paquet A (2009).
<em>goTools: Functions for Gene Ontology database</em>.
R package version 1.48.0. 
</p>

---------
gpls
<p>Ding B (2016).
<em>gpls: Classification using generalized partial least squares</em>.
R package version 1.46.0. 
</p>

---------
gprege
<p>Kalaitzis AA and Lawrence ND (2011).
&ldquo;A Simple Approach to Ranking Differentially Expressed Gene Expression Time Courses through Gaussian Process Regression.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>, <b>12</b>(180).
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1186/1471-2105-12-180">doi: 10.1186/1471-2105-12-180</a>, <a href="http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/12/180">http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/12/180</a>. 
</p>

---------
gQTLBase
<p>Carey V (2016).
<em>gQTLBase: gQTLBase: infrastructure for eQTL, mQTL and similar studies</em>.
R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

---------
gQTLstats
<p>Carey V (2016).
<em>gQTLstats: gQTLstats: computationally efficient analysis for eQTL and
allied studies</em>.
R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

---------
graph
<p>Gentleman R, Whalen E, Huber W and Falcon S (2016).
<em>graph: graph: A package to handle graph data structures</em>.
R package version 1.52.0. 
</p>

---------
GraphAlignment
<p>Berg J and Laessig M (2006).
&ldquo;Cross-species analysis of biological networks by Bayesian alignment.&rdquo;
<em>PNAS</em>, <b>103</b>(29), pp. -5. 
</p>

---------
GraphAT
<p>Balasubramanian R, LaFramboise T and Scholtens D (2012).
<em>GraphAT: Graph Theoretic Association Tests</em>.
R package version 1.46.0. 
</p>

---------
graphite
<p>Sales G, Calura E and Romualdi C (2016).
<em>graphite: GRAPH Interaction from pathway Topological Environment</em>.
R package version 1.20.1. 
</p>

---------
GraphPAC
<p>Ryslik G and Zhao H (2012).
<em>GraphPAC: Identification of Mutational Clusters in Proteins via a Graph
Theoretical Approach.</em>.
R package version 1.16.0. 
</p>

---------
GRENITS
<p>Morrissey E (2012).
<em>GRENITS: Gene Regulatory Network Inference Using Time Series</em>.
R package version 1.26.0. 
</p>

---------
GreyListChIP
<p>Brown G (2015).
<em>GreyListChIP: Grey Lists &ndash; Mask Artefact Regions Based on ChIP Inputs</em>.
R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

---------
GRmetrics
<p>Clark N (2016).
<em>GRmetrics: Calculate growth-rate inhibition (GR) metrics</em>.
R package version 1.0.0, <a href="https://github.com/uc-bd2k/GRmetrics">https://github.com/uc-bd2k/GRmetrics</a>. 
</p>

---------
groHMM
<p>Chae M, Danko CG and Kraus WL (2015).
&ldquo;groHMM: a computational tool for identifying unannotated and cell type-specific transcription units from  
global run-on sequencing data.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>, <b>16</b>(222). 
</p>

---------
GSALightning
<p>Chang BHW (2015).
<em>GSALightning: Fast Permutation-based Gene Set Analysis</em>.
R package version 1.2.0, <a href="https://github.com/billyhw/GSALightning">https://github.com/billyhw/GSALightning</a>. 
</p>

---------
GSAR
<p>Rahmatallah Y, Emmert-Streib F and Glazko G (2014).
&ldquo;Gene sets net correlations analysis (GSNCA): a multivariate differential coexpression test for gene sets.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>30</b>, pp. 360-368. 
</p>

<p>Rahmatallah Y, Emmert-Streib F and Glazko G (2012).
&ldquo;Gene set analysis for self-contained tests: complex null and specific alternative hypotheses.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>28</b>, pp. 3073-3080. 
</p>

---------
GSCA

<em>Nucleic Acids Res. gkv873</em>. 
</p>

R package version 1.36.0. 
</p>

R package version 1.34.0. 
</p>

R package version 1.8.0.

---------
lpsymphony
<p>Kim V (2016).
<em>lpsymphony: Symphony integer linear programming solver in R</em>.
http://R-Forge.R-project.org/projects/rsymphony,
https://projects.coin-or.org/SYMPHONY,
http://www.coin-or.org/download/source/SYMPHONY/. 
</p>

---------
lumi
<p>Du, P., Kibbe, W.A., Lin and S.M. (2008).
&ldquo;lumi: a pipeline for processing Illumina microarray.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>. 
</p>

<p>P D, X Z, CC H, N J, WA K, L H and SM L (2010).
&ldquo;Comparison of Beta-value and M-value methods for quantifying methylation levels by microarray analysis.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>. 
</p>

<p>Lin, S.M., Du, P., Kibbe and W.A. (2008).
&ldquo;Model-based Variance-stabilizing Transformation for Illumina Microarray Data.&rdquo;
<em>Nucleic Acids Res</em>. 
</p>

<p>Du, P., Kibbe, W.A., Lin and S.M. (2007).
&ldquo;nuID: A universal naming schema of oligonucleotides for Illumina, Affymetrix, and other microarrays.&rdquo;
<em>Biology Direct</em>. 
</p>

---------
LVSmiRNA
<p>Calza S, Chen S and Pawitan Y (2015).
<em>LVSmiRNA: LVS normalization for Agilent miRNA data</em>.
R package version 1.24.0. 
</p>

---------
LymphoSeq
<p>Coffey D (2016).
<em>LymphoSeq: Analyze high-throughput sequencing of T and B cell receptors</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
M3D
<p>Mayo T (2016).
<em>M3D: Identifies differentially methylated regions across testing
groups</em>.
R package version 1.8.0. 
</p>

---------
M3Drop
<p>Andrews T (2016).
<em>M3Drop: Michaelis-Menten Modelling of Dropouts in single-cell RNASeq</em>.
R package version 1.0.0, <a href="https://github.com/tallulandrews/M3Drop">https://github.com/tallulandrews/M3Drop</a>. 
</p>

---------
maanova
<p>Wu H, Yang mbH, Churchill KSwifG, Kerr K and Cui. X (2016).
<em>maanova: Tools for analyzing Micro Array experiments</em>.
R package version 1.44.0, <a href="http://research.jax.org/faculty/churchill">http://research.jax.org/faculty/churchill</a>. 
</p>

---------
macat
<p>Toedling J, Schmeier S, Heinig M, Georgi B and Roepcke S (2005).
&ldquo;macat - microarray chromosomal analysis tool.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>21</b>(9), pp. 2112&ndash;2113. 
</p>

---------
maCorrPlot
<p>Ploner A (2016).
<em>maCorrPlot: Visualize artificial correlation in microarray data</em>.
R package version 1.44.0, <a href="http://www.pubmedcentral.gov/articlerender.fcgi?tool=pubmed&amp;pubmedid=15799785">http://www.pubmedcentral.gov/articlerender.fcgi?tool=pubmed&amp;pubmedid=15799785</a>. 
</p>

---------
made4
<p>AC C, J T, G P and DG H (2005).
&ldquo;MADE4:an R package for multivariate analysis of gene expression data.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>21(11)</b>, pp. 2789-90. 
</p>

---------
MADSEQ
<p>Kong Y, Auton A and Greally JM (2016).
<em>MADSEQ: Mosaic Aneuploidy Detection and Quantification using Massive
Parallel Sequencing Data</em>.
R package version 1.0.0, <a href="https://github.com/ykong2/MADSEQ">https://github.com/ykong2/MADSEQ</a>. 
</p>

---------
maftools
<p>Mayakonda A and Koeffler PH (2016).
&ldquo;Maftools: Efficient analysis, visualization and summarization of MAF files from large-scale cohort based cancer studies.&rdquo;
<em>BioRxiv</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1101/052662">doi: 10.1101/052662</a>. 
</p>

---------
maigesPack
<p>Esteves GH, Hirata Jr wcfR, Neves EJ, Cristo EB, Simoes AC and Fahham L (2016).
<em>maigesPack: Functions to handle cDNA microarray data, including several
methods of data analysis</em>.
R package version 1.38.0, <a href="http://www.maiges.org/en/software/">http://www.maiges.org/en/software/</a>. 
</p>

---------
MAIT
<p>Fernandez-Albert, Francesc, Llorach, Rafael, Andres-Lacueva, Cristina, Perera and Alexandre (2014).
&ldquo;An R package to analyse LC/MS metabolomic data: MAIT (Metabolite Automatic Identification Toolkit).&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics (Oxford, England)</em>, <b>30</b>(13), pp. 1937&ndash;1939.
ISSN 1367-4811, <a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btu136">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btu136</a>, <a href="http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/cgi/content/long/30/13/1937">http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/cgi/content/long/30/13/1937</a>. 
</p>

---------
makecdfenv
<p>Irizarry RA, Gautier L, Huber W and Bolstad B (2006).
<em>makecdfenv: CDF Environment Maker</em>.
R package version 1.50.0. 
</p>

---------
MANOR
<p>Neuvial P and Hupe P (2015).
<em>MANOR: CGH Micro-Array NORmalization</em>.
R package version 1.46.0, <a href="http://bioinfo.curie.fr/projects/manor/index.html">http://bioinfo.curie.fr/projects/manor/index.html</a>. 
</p>

---------
manta

---------
MantelCorr
<p>Steinmeyer B and Shannon W (2016).
<em>MantelCorr: Compute Mantel Cluster Correlations</em>.
R package version 1.44.0. 
</p>

---------
maPredictDSC
<p>Tarca AL (2013).
<em>maPredictDSC: Phenotype prediction using microarray data: approach of the best
overall team in the IMPROVER Diagnostic Signature Challenge</em>.
R package version 1.12.0, <a href="http://bioinformaticsprb.med.wayne.edu/maPredictDSC">http://bioinformaticsprb.med.wayne.edu/maPredictDSC</a>. 
</p>

---------
marray
<p>Paquet YHYwcfA and Dudoit. S (2009).
<em>marray: Exploratory analysis for two-color spotted microarray data</em>.
R package version 1.52.0, <a href="http://www.maths.usyd.edu.au/u/jeany/">http://www.maths.usyd.edu.au/u/jeany/</a>. 
</p>

---------
maSigPro
<p>Conesa A and Nueda MJ (2016).
<em>maSigPro: Significant Gene Expression Profile Differences in Time Course
Gene Expression Data</em>.
R package version 1.46.0, <a href="http://bioinfo.cipf.es/">http://bioinfo.cipf.es/</a>. 
</p>

---------
maskBAD
<p>M D, A. L, I. H, P. K and M. L (2009).
&ldquo;The effects of probe binding affinity differences on gene expression measurements and how to deal with them.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>25</b>, pp. 2772&ndash;2779. 
</p>

<p>M D, M. L and A. L (2012).
&ldquo;'maskBAD' - a package to detect and remove Affymetrix probes with binding affinity differences.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>, <b>13</b>, pp. 56. 
</p>

---------
MassArray
<p>Thompson RF and Greally JM (2009).
<em>MassArray: Analytical Tools for MassArray Data</em>.
R package version 1.26.0. 
</p>

---------
massiR
<p>Buckberry S, Bent S, Bianco-Miotto T and Roberts C (2014).
&ldquo;massiR: a method for predicting the sex of samples in gene expression microarray datasets.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btu161">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btu161</a>, <a href="http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2014/03/22/bioinformatics.btu161">http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2014/03/22/bioinformatics.btu161</a>. 
</p>

---------
MassSpecWavelet
<p>Du P, Kibbe WA and Lin SM (2006).
&ldquo;Improved peak detection in mass spectrum by incorporating continuous wavelet transform-based pattern matching.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>22</b>, pp. 2059-2065. 
</p>

---------
MAST
<p>McDavid A, Finak G and Yajima M (2016).
<em>MAST: Model-based Analysis of Single Cell Transcriptomics</em>.
R package version 1.0.5, <a href="https://github.com/RGLab/MAST/">https://github.com/RGLab/MAST/</a>. 
</p>

---------
matchBox
<p>Ross AE, Luigi M, Milena V, Chris C, Jinshui F, David M B and Edward M S (2011).
&ldquo;Gene expression pathways of high grade localized prostate cancer.&rdquo;
<em>The Prostate</em>, pp. 1&ndash;11.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1002/pros.21373">doi: 10.1002/pros.21373</a>. 
</p>

<p>Irizarry RA, Daniel W, Forrest S, Irene F K, Shyam B, Bryan C F, Edward G, Joe G N G, Joel G, Gregory G, Constance G, Sara C H, Eric H, Anne E J, Ernest K, Francisco M, Laura M, Hannah L, David P, John Q, Alan S, Michael W, Yanqin Y, Shui Qing Y and Wayne Y (2005).
&ldquo;Multiple-laboratory comparison of microarray platforms.&rdquo;
<em>Nat. Genet.</em>, <b>2</b>(5), pp. 345&ndash;350.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1038/nmeth756">doi: 10.1038/nmeth756</a>. 
</p>

---------
MatrixRider
<p>Grassi E (2015).
<em>MatrixRider: Obtain total affinity and occupancies for binding site matrices
on a given sequence</em>.
R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

---------
matter
<p>Bemis KA (2016).
<em>matter: A framework for rapid prototyping with binary data on disk</em>.
R package version 1.0.0, <a href="http://www.cardinalmsi.org">http://www.cardinalmsi.org</a>. 
</p>

MBAmethyl
<p>Wang T, Chen M and Zhao H (2014).
&ldquo;Extracting DNA methylation values by joint modeling of multiple profiles.&rdquo;
<em>Under review</em>. 
</p>

---------
MBASED
<p>Mayba O and Gilbert H (2014).

R package version 1.8.0. 
</p>

---------
MBCB
<p>Xie Y (2010).
<em>MBCB: MBCB (Model-based Background Correction for Beadarray)</em>.
R package version 1.28.0, <a href="http://www.utsouthwestern.edu">http://www.utsouthwestern.edu</a>.

---------
mBPCR
<p>Rancoita P and Hutter wcfM (2016).

MBttest

<em>MBttest: Multiple Beta t-Tests</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
mcaGUI
<p>Copeland WK, Krishnan V, Beck D, Settles M, Foster J, Day KCM, Hickey R, Schutte UM, Zhou X, Williams C, Forney LJ and Noel ZAPMGbcbJVwcbY (2016).
<em>mcaGUI: Microbial Community Data Analysis GUI</em>.
Initiative for Bioinformatics and Evolutionary Studies (IBEST), University of Idaho,
Moscow ID, 83844. 
</p>

---------
MCRestimate
<p>Johannes M, Ruschhaupt M, Froehlich H, Mansmann U, Buness A, Warnat P, Huber W, Benner A and Beissbarth T (2016).
<em>MCRestimate: Misclassification error estimation with cross-validation</em>.
R package version 2.30.0. 
</p>

---------
mdgsa
<p>Montaner D and Dopazo J (2010).
&ldquo;Multidimensional Gene Set Analysis of Genomic Data.&rdquo;
<em>PLoS One</em>, <b>5</b>(4), pp. e10348.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1371/journal.pone.0010348">doi: 10.1371/journal.pone.0010348</a>, <a href="http://www.plosone.org/article/info%3Adoi%2F10.1371%2Fjournal.pone.0010348}.">http://www.plosone.org/article/info%3Adoi%2F10.1371%2Fjournal.pone.0010348}.</a></p>

---------
mdqc
<p>Harrington J (2008).
<em>mdqc: Mahalanobis Distance Quality Control for microarrays</em>.
R package version 1.36.0. 
</p>

---------
MEAL
<p>Ruiz C, Hernandez-Ferrer C and Gonz&lt;c3&gt;&lt;a1&gt;lez J (2016).
<em>MEAL: Perform methylation analysis</em>.
R package version 1.4.2. 
</p>

MeasurementError.cor

R package version 1.46.0.

---------
MEIGOR
<p>Egea J, Henriques D, Villaverde AF and Cokelaer T (2012).
<em>MEIGOR: MEIGO - MEtaheuristics for bIoinformatics Global Optimization</em>.
R package version 1.8.0. 
</p>

---------
MergeMaid
<p>&lt;gp@jhu.edu&gt; XZLC&lt;EG&lt;GP (2007).
<em>MergeMaid: Merge Maid</em>.
R package version 2.46.0, <a href="http://astor.som.jhmi.edu/MergeMaid">http://astor.som.jhmi.edu/MergeMaid</a>. 
</p>

---------
Mergeomics
<p>Makinen V, Le Shu, Zhao Y, Kurt Z, Zhang B and Yang X (2016).
<em>Mergeomics: Integrative network analysis of omics data</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
MeSHDbi
<p>Tsuyuzaki K, Morota G, Ishii M, Nakazato T, Miyazaki S and Nikaido I (2015).
&ldquo;MeSH ORA framework: R/Bioconductor packages to support MeSH over-representation analysis.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1186/s12859-015-0453-z">doi: 10.1186/s12859-015-0453-z</a>, <a href="http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/16/45">http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/16/45</a>. 
</p>

---------
meshes
<p>Yu G (2016).
<em>meshes: MeSH Enrichment and Semantic analyses</em>.
R package version 1.0.0, <a href="https://guangchuangyu.github.io/meshes">https://guangchuangyu.github.io/meshes</a>. 
</p>

---------
meshr
<p>Tsuyuzaki K, Morota G, Ishii M, Nakazato T, Miyazaki S and Nikaido I (2015).
&ldquo;MeSH ORA framework: R/Bioconductor packages to support MeSH over-representation analysis.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1186/s12859-015-0453-z">doi: 10.1186/s12859-015-0453-z</a>, <a href="http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/16/45">http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/16/45</a>. 
</p>

<p>Morota G, Penagaricano F, Petersen JL, Ciobanu D, Tsuyuzaki K and Nikaido I (2015).
&ldquo;An application of MeSH enrichment analysis in livestock.&rdquo;
<em>Animal Genetics</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1111/age.12307">doi: 10.1111/age.12307</a>, <a href="http://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/10.1111/age.12307/abstract">http://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/10.1111/age.12307/abstract</a>. 
</p>

---------
MeSHSim
<p>Zhou J and Shui Y (2015).
<em>MeSHSim: MeSH(Medical Subject Headings) Semantic Similarity Measures</em>.
R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

---------
messina
<p>Pinese M, Scarlett CJ, Kench JG, Colvin EK, Segara D, Henshall SM, Sutherland RL and Biankin AV (2009).
&ldquo;Messina: A Novel Analysis Tool to Identify Biologically Relevant Molecules in Disease.&rdquo;
<em>PLoS ONE</em>, <b>4</b>(4), pp. e5337.
ISSN 1932-6203, <a href="http://doi.org/%7B10.1371/journal.pone.0005337%7D">doi: 10.1371/journal.pone.0005337</a>, <a href="%7Bhttp://dx.doi.org/10.1371/journal.pone.0005337%7D">{http://dx.doi.org/10.1371/journal.pone.0005337}</a>. 
</p>

---------
metaArray
<p>&lt;hyung_won_choi@nuhs.edu.sg&gt; DGHC (2016).
<em>metaArray: Integration of Microarray Data for Meta-analysis</em>.
R package version 1.52.0. 
</p>

---------
Metab
<p>Aggio R, Villas-Boas SG and Ruggiero K (2011).
&ldquo;Metab: an R package for high-throughput analysis of metabolomics data generated by GC-MS.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics Journal</em>, pp. 2316-2318.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btr379">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btr379</a>, <a href="http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/27/16/2316.short">http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/27/16/2316.short</a>. 
</p>

---------
metabomxtr
<p>Nodzenski M, Reisetter A and Scholtens D (2016).
<em>metabomxtr: A package to run mixture models for truncated metabolomics data
with normal or lognormal distributions</em>.
R package version 1.8.0. 
</p>

---------
MetaboSignal
<p>Rodriguez-Martinez A, Ayala R, Posma JM, Neves AL and Dumas M (2016).
<em>MetaboSignal: MetaboSignal: a network-based approach to overlay and explore
metabolic and signaling KEGG pathways</em>.
R package version 1.4.0. 
</p>

---------
metaCCA
<p>Anna Cichonska, Juho Rousu, Pekka Marttinen, Antti J Kangas, Pasi Soininen, Terho Lehtimaki, Olli T Raitakari, Marjo-Riitta Jarvelin, Veikko Salomaa, Mika Ala-Korpela, Samuli Ripatti and Matti Pirinen (2016).
&ldquo;metaCCA: Summary statistics-based multivariate meta-analysis
of genome-wide association studies using canonical correlation analysis.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>btw052</b>. 
</p>

---------
metagene
<p>Beauparlant CJ, Lamaze FC, Samb R, Deschenes AL and Droit. A (2014).
<em>metagene: A package to produce metagene plots</em>.
R package version 2.6.1. 
</p>

---------
metagenomeFeatures
<p>Olson ND, Paulson JN and Bravo HC (2016).
<em>metagenomeFeatures: Exploration of marker-gene sequence taxonomic annotations</em>.
R package version 1.4.0, <a href="https://github.com/HCBravoLab/metagenomeFeatures">https://github.com/HCBravoLab/metagenomeFeatures</a>. 
</p>

metagenomeSeq

metahdep
<p>Stevens JR and Nicholas G (2011).
<em>metahdep: Hierarchical Dependence in Meta-Analysis</em>.
R package version 1.32.0. 
</p>

metaMS
<p>Wehrens R, Weingart G and Mattivi F (2014).
&ldquo;metaMS: An open-source pipeline for GC-MS-based untargeted metabolomics.&rdquo;
<em>J. Chrom. B</em>, <b>966</b>, pp. 109-116. 
</p>

---------
metaSeq
<p>Tsuyuzaki K and Nikaido I (2013).
<em>metaSeq: Meta-analysis of RNA-Seq count data in multiple studies</em>.
R package version 1.14.0. 
</p>

---------
metaseqR
<p>Moulos P and Hatzis P (2014).
&ldquo;Systematic integration of RNA-Seq statistical algorithms for accurate detection of differential gene expression patterns.&rdquo;
<em>Nucleic Acids Research</em>.
(Version 1.5.14), <a href="http://nar.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2014/12/01/nar.gku1273.abstract">http://nar.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2014/12/01/nar.gku1273.abstract</a>. 
</p>

---------
MetCirc
<p>Naake T and Gaquerel E (2016).
<em>MetCirc: MetCirc - a workflow to analyse and visualise metabolomics data</em>.
R package version 1.0.0. 
</p>

---------
MethPed
<p>Ahamed M, Danielsson A, Nemes S and CarÃ©n H (2016).
<em>MethPed: A DNA methylation classifier tool for the identification of
pediatric brain tumor subtypes</em>.
R package version 1.2.0. 
</p>

---------
MethTargetedNGS
<p>Frohlich MAJwCoPH and El-Maarri PDO (2015).
<em>MethTargetedNGS: Perform Methylation Analysis on Next Generation Sequencing Data</em>.
R package version 1.6.0. 
</p>

---------
methVisual
<p>Zackay A and Steinhoff C (2016).
<em>methVisual: Methods for visualization and statistics on DNA methylation data</em>.
R package version 1.26.0. 
</p>

---------
methyAnalysis
<p>Du P and Bourgon R (2016).
<em>methyAnalysis: DNA methylation data analysis and visualization</em>.
R package version 1.16.0. 
</p>

---------
MethylAid
<p>van Iterson M, Tobi EW, Slieker RC, den Hollander W, Luijk R, Slagboom PE and Heijmans BT (2014).
&ldquo;MethylAid: Visual and interactive quality control of large Illumina 450k data sets.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>30</b>.
<a href="http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/30/23/3435">http://bioinformatics.oxfordjournals.org/content/30/23/3435</a>. 
</p>

---------
methylKit
<p>Akalin A, Kormaksson M, Li S, Garrett-Bakelman FE, Figueroa ME, Melnick A and Mason CE (2012).
&ldquo;methylKit: a comprehensive R package for the
analysis of genome-wide DNA methylation profiles.&rdquo;
<em>Genome Biology</em>, <b>13</b>(10), pp. R87. 
</p>

---------
MethylMix
<p>Gevaert O (2014).
<em>MethylMix: MethylMix: Identifying methylation driven cancer genes.</em>.
R package version 1.8.0. 
</p>

---------
methylMnM
<p>Zhou Y, Zhang B, Lin N, Zhang B and Wang T (2013).
<em>methylMnM: detect different methylation level (DMR)</em>.
R package version 1.12.0. 
</p>

---------
methylPipe
<p>Kishore K, de Pretis S, Lister R, Morelli MJ, Bianchi V, Amati B, Ecker JR and Pelizzola M (2015).
&ldquo;methylPipe and compEpiTools: a suite of R packages for the integrative analysis of epigenomics data.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1186/s12859-015-0742-6">doi: 10.1186/s12859-015-0742-6</a>. 
</p>

---------
MethylSeekR
<p>Burger L, Gaidatzis D, Schubeler D and Stadler MB (2013).
&ldquo;Identification of active regulatory regions from DNA methylation data.&rdquo;
<em>Nucleic Acids Research</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/nar/gkt599">doi: 10.1093/nar/gkt599</a>, <a href="http://nar.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2013/07/04/nar.gkt599.long">http://nar.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2013/07/04/nar.gkt599.long</a>. 
</p>

---------
methylumi
<p>Davis S, Du P, Bilke S, Triche, Jr. T and Bootwalla M (2016).
<em>methylumi: Handle Illumina methylation data</em>.
R package version 2.20.0. 
</p>

---------
Mfuzz
<p>Futschik M and Carlisle B (2005).
&ldquo;Noise robust clustering of gene expression time-course data.&rdquo;
<em>Journal of Bioinformatics and Computational Biology</em>, pp.  965-988.
<a href="http://mfuzz.sysbiolab.eu">http://mfuzz.sysbiolab.eu</a>. 
</p>

<p>Kumar L and Futschik M (2007).
&ldquo;Mfuzz: a software package for soft clustering of microarray data.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformation</em>, pp. 5-7
.
<a href="http://mfuzz.sysbiolab.eu">http://mfuzz.sysbiolab.eu</a>. 
</p>

---------
MGFM
<p>Amrani KE (2014).
<em>MGFM: Marker Gene Finder in Microarray gene expression data</em>.
R package version 1.8.0. 
</p>

---------
MGFR
<p>Amrani KE (2016).
<em>MGFR: Marker Gene Finder in RNA-seq data</em>.
R package version 1.0.0. 
</p>

---------
mgsa
<p>Bauer S and Gagneur J (2016).
<em>mgsa: Model-based gene set analysis</em>.
R package version 1.22.0, <a href="https://github.com/sba1/mgsa-bioc">https://github.com/sba1/mgsa-bioc</a>. 
</p>

---------
MiChip
<p>Blake J (2009).
<em>MiChip: MiChip Parsing and Summarizing Functions</em>.
R package version 1.28.0. 
</p>

---------
microRNA
<p>Gentleman R and Falcon S (2016).
<em>microRNA: Data and functions for dealing with microRNAs</em>.
R package version 1.32.0. 
</p>

---------
MIMOSA
<p>Finak G, McDavid A, Chattopadhyay P, Dominguez M, De Rosa SC, Roederer M and Gottardo R (2013).
&ldquo;Mixture models for single-cell assays with applications to vaccine studies.&rdquo;
<em>Biostatistics</em>.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/biostatistics/kxt024">doi: 10.1093/biostatistics/kxt024</a>, http://biostatistics.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2013/07/24/biostatistics.kxt024.full.pdf+html, <a href="http://biostatistics.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2013/07/24/biostatistics.kxt024.abstract">http://biostatistics.oxfordjournals.org/content/early/2013/07/24/biostatistics.kxt024.abstract</a>. 
</p>

---------
MineICA
<p>Biton A (2012).
<em>MineICA: Analysis of an ICA decomposition obtained on genomics data</em>.
R package version 1.14.0. 
</p>

---------
minet
<p>Meyer PE, Lafitte F and Bontempi G (2008).
&ldquo;MINET: An open source R/Bioconductor Package for Mutual Information based Network Inference.&rdquo;
<em>BMC Bioinformatics</em>, <b>9</b>.
<a href="http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/9/461">http://www.biomedcentral.com/1471-2105/9/461</a>. 
</p>

---------
minfi
<p>Aryee MJ, Jaffe AE, Corrada-Bravo H, Ladd-Acosta C, Feinberg AP, Hansen KD and Irizarry RA (2014).
&ldquo;Minfi: A flexible and comprehensive Bioconductor package for the analysis of Infinium DNA Methylation microarrays.&rdquo;
<em>Bioinformatics</em>, <b>30</b>(10), pp. 1363&ndash;1369.
<a href="http://doi.org/10.1093/bioinformatics/btu049">doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btu049</a>. 
</p>

<p>Maksimovic J, Gordon L and Oshlack A (2012).
